Make your nutritionist happy and lets get dirty on the chopping board! After a recent visit to my nutritionist, who encouraged me to incorporate more cooked vegetables into my meals, I was inspired to create something truly special. Enter the Vegan Kale and Roasted Beet Salad - a vibrant medley of earthy sweetness and energizing flavors, perfectly suited for summer&#039;s light and fresh fare. 🌿✨ 

I&#039;ve always been a fan of beets, especially cooked, giving their unique earthy sweetness and the energizing boost they provide. So, I set out to craft a salad that beautifully combines the richness of roasted beets with the crispness of kale. The result is a symphony of textures and colors, a true celebration of seasonal abundance.

Looking for a quick, nutritious, and flavorful summer dish? Try this amazing Beans and Swiss Chard recipe! 🍽️🌞 

👉 Ingredients: Chopped garlic, Cooked white beans, tomatoes, Swiss chard, olive oil, lemon, cumin, salt, black pepper. 

👉 Easy Preparation: Sauté garlic, add beans, tomatoes, Swiss chard, and seasoning. Cook until tender. Voila! A tasty and wholesome meal is ready! 

👉 Nutrient Powerhouse: Packed with plant-based protein, fiber, vitamins A, K, C, iron, and magnesium. Fuel your body with goodness! 

👉 Versatile Serving: I enjoyed it on vegan labane and fresh baked focaccia. But you can serve it with hummus, vegan yogurt, or get creative with your favorite toppings!

Building a brand is such a long hard journey and sometimes it feels like I&#039;m just a dreamer, and it won&#039;t work..and then you get this, to remind yourself to keep going,  your in the right track. 

Thank you so much for all the birthday wishes and love ❤️ . Thanks a lot for those who are showing interest, follow, comment and likes,it doesn&#039;t go unnoticed!

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Vegan Tomatoes Tart Tatin! 🍅😘 

It&#039;s about time to</span>
						<svg style="color: rgba(255,255,255,1)" class="svg-inline--fa fa-play fa-w-14 sbi_playbtn" aria-label="Play" aria-hidden="true" data-fa-processed="" data-prefix="fa" data-icon="play" role="presentation" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512"><path fill="currentColor" d="M424.4 214.7L72.4 6.6C43.8-10.3 0 6.1 0 47.9V464c0 37.5 40.7 60.1 72.4 41.3l352-208c31.4-18.5 31.5-64.1 0-82.6z"></path></svg>			<img decoding="async" src="https://cacao-shamaness.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="Vegan Tomatoes Tart Tatin! 🍅😘 

It&#039;s about time to share this wonderful easy recipe for your next brunch or for our lovely spring holiday Shavuot 

I decided to veganise this Tart Tatin version and added Lovely Vegan Truffle Cashew Mozzarella by @plenty_4u  which I use their vegan cheese on a regular basis. 

This is the perfect shareable appetizer, on your next brunch gathering table. Candied cherry tomatoes Tart  with savory cheese oozing after a good broil in the oven.
a seriously must try
